185→\n   186→\n   187→def _extract_injectable_params(\n   188→    tree: ast.Module, file_path: str\n   189→) -> list[tuple[str, str, int]]:\n   190→    \"\"\"Extract Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n   191→\n   192→    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n   193→    \"\"\"\n   194→    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n   195→\n   196→    for            continue\n   207→                annotation = arg.annotation\n   208→                if annotation is None:\n   209→                    continue\n   210→\n   211→                # Check for \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n   225→    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n   226→    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n   227→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n   228→            slice_val = annotation.slice\n   229→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   230→                return True\n   231→            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n   232→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n   233→                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n   234→                    return True\n   235→        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n   236→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n   237→            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n   238→                slice_val = annotation.slice\n   239→                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   240→                    return True\n   241→\n   242→    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n   243→    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n   244→        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n   245→        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n   246→                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n   247→            return True\n   248→        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n   249→                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n   250→            return True\n   251→\n   252→    return False\n   253→\n   254→\n   255→def _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n   256→    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n   257→    args = func_def.args\n   258→    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n   259→    all_args = args.args\n   260→    defaults = args.defaults\n   261→\n   262→    if not defaults:\n   263→        return False\n   264→\n   265→    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n   266→    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n   267→    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n   268→        if arg is target_arg:\n   269→            default_idx = i - offset\n   270→            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n   271→                default = defaults[default_idx]\n   272→                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n   273→    return False\n   274→\n   275→\n   276→def _find_wiring_call_sites(\n   277→    param_name: str,\n   278→    class_name: str,\n   279→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n   280→) -> bool:\n   281→    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n   282→    for tree in trees.values():\n   283→        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   284→            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n   285→                # Check keyword arguments\n   286→                for kw in node.keywords:\n   287→                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n   288→                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n   289→                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n   290→                            return True\n   291→    return False\n   292→\n   293→\n   294→def _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n   295→    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n   296→    func = call.func\n   297→    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n   298→        return True\n   299→    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n   300→        return True\n   301→    return False\n   302→\n   303→\n   304→def analyze_unwired_callables(\n   305→    config: WiringConfig,\n   306→    source_dir: Path,\n   307→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   308→    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n   309→\n   310→    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n   311→    1. invariant: category sums == severity sums == total.\n    Blocking count is derived from rollout_mode per OQ-6.\n\n    Attributes:\n        target_dir: Root directory that was analyzed.\n        files_analyzed: Number of Python files successfully parsed.\n        files_skipped: Number of files excluded or unparseable (OQ-2).\n        unwired_callables: Findings from unwired callable analysis (G-001).\n        orphan_modules: Findings from orphan module analysis (G-002).\n        unwired_registries: Findings from registry analysis (G-003).\n        scan_duration_seconds: Wall-clock time of analysis run.\n        rollout_mode: Active rollout mode for blocking semantics.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    target_dir: str = \"\"\n    files_analyzed: int = 0\n    files_skipped: int = 0\n    unwired_callables: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    orphan_modules: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    unwired_registries: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    scan_duration_seconds: float = 0.0\n    rollout_mode: str = \"shadow\"\n\n    @property\n    def all_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n        \"\"\"All findings across all categories.\"\"\"\n        return self.unwired_callables + self.orphan_modules + self.unwired_registries\n\n    @property\n    def total_findings(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Total finding count (category sum invariant).\"\"\"\n        return len(self.all_findings)\n\n    @property\n    def unsuppressed_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n        \"\"\"Findings not suppressed by whitelist.\"\"\"\n        return [f for f in self.all_findings if not f.suppressed]\n\n    @property\n    def clean(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"True if zero unsuppressed findings regardless of rollout mode.\"\"\"\n        return len(self.unsuppressed_findings) == 0\n\n    def blocking_count(self, mode: str | None = None) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Count of findings that block the gate for the given rollout mode.\n\n        Args:\n            mode: Override rollout mode. Uses self.rollout_mode if None.\n\n        Returns:\n            Number of blocking findings per OQ-6:\n            - shadow: 0 (never blocks)\n            - soft: critical unsuppressed only\n            - full: critical + major unsuppressed\n        \"\"\"\n        effective_mode = mode or self.rollout_mode\n        unsuppressed = self.unsuppressed_findings\n\n        if effective_mode == \"shadow\":\n            return 0\n        elif effective_mode == \"soft\":\n            return sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n        else:  # full\n            return sum(\n                1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity in (\"critical\", \"major\")\n            )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Analyzers (sections 5.2.1, 5.2.2, 5.2.3)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _collect_python_files(\n    source_dir: Path,\n    exclude_patterns: list[str],\n) -> tuple[list[Path], int]:\n    \"\"\"Collect Python files from source_dir, applying exclude patterns.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (included files, skipped count).\n    \"\"\"\n    included: list[Path] = []\n    skipped = 0\n\n    for py_file in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*.py\")):\n        name = py_file.name\n        if any(fnmatch(name, pat) for pat in exclude_patterns):\n            skipped += 1\n            continue\n        included.append(py_file)\n\n    return included, skipped\n\n\ndef _safe_parse(file_path: Path) -> ast.Module | None:\n    \"\"\"Parse a Python file, returning None on SyntaxError (R2 mitigation).\"\"\"\n    try:\n        source = file_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        return ast.parse(source, filename=str(file_path))\n    except SyntaxError as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"SyntaxError parsing %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n    except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"Cannot read %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n\n\ndef _apply_whitelist(\n    findings: list[WiringFinding],\n    whitelist: list[WhitelistEntry],\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Mark findings as suppressed if they match a whitelist entry.\"\"\"\n    suppressed_symbols = {\n        (e.symbol, e.finding_type) for e in whitelist\n    }\n    for finding in findings:\n        if (finding.symbol_name, finding.finding_type) in suppressed_symbols:\n            finding.suppressed = True\n            finding.severity = \"info\"\n    return findings\n\n\n# --- G-001: Unwired Callable Analysis (section 5.2.1) ---\n\n\ndef _extract_injectable_params(\n    tree: ast.Module, file_path: str\n) -> list[tuple[str, str, int]]:\n    \"\"\"Extract Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n\n    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n    \"\"\"\n    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if not isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            continue\n\n        for item in node.body:\n            if not isinstance(item, ast.FunctionDef) or item.name != \"__init__\":\n                continue\n\n            for arg in item.args.args:\n                if arg.arg == \"self\":\n                    continue\n                annotation = arg.annotation\n                if annotation is None:\n                    continue\n\n                # Check for Optional[Callable] or Callable | None\n                if _is_optional_callable(annotation):\n                    # Verify default is None\n                    if _has_none_default(item, arg):\n                        symbol = f\"{node.name}.{arg.arg}\"\n                        injectables.append(\n                            (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n                        )\n\n    return injectables\n\n\ndef _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n            slice_val = annotation.slice\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                return True\n            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n                slice_val = annotation.slice\n                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n\n    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n            return True\n        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n            return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n    args = func_def.args\n    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n    all_args = args.args\n    defaults = args.defaults\n\n    if not defaults:\n        return False\n\n    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n        if arg is target_arg:\n            default_idx = i - offset\n            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n                default = defaults[default_idx]\n                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n    return False\n\n\ndef _find_wiring_call_sites(\n    param_name: str,\n    class_name: str,\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n    for tree in trees.values():\n        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                # Check keyword arguments\n                for kw in node.keywords:\n                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n                            return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n    func = call.func\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n        return True\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_unwired_callables(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n    1. Parse all Python files, extract Optional[Callable] constructor params\n    2. For each injectable, search all files for keyword call sites\n    3. If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n    4. Apply whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_callable\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        injectables = _extract_injectable_params(tree, str(file_path))\n        for symbol, param_name, lineno in injectables:\n            class_name = symbol.split(\".\")[0]\n            if not _find_wiring_call_sites(param_name, class_name, trees):\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"unwired_callable\",\n                        file_path=str(file_path),\n                        symbol_name=symbol,\n                        line_number=lineno,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Parameter '{param_name}' typed Optional[Callable] \"\n                            f\"with default None is never wired by any call site\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"critical\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-002: Orphan Module Analysis (section 5.2.2) ---\n\n\ndef _find_provider_dirs(source_dir: Path, provider_names: frozenset[str]) -> list[Path]:\n    \"\"\"Find directories matching provider_dir_names convention.\"\"\"\n    providers: list[Path] = []\n    for d in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*\")):\n        if d.is_dir() and d.name in provider_names:\n            providers.append(d)\n    return providers\n\n\ndef _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> set[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract all imported module/symbol names from an AST.\"\"\"\n    imports: set[str] = set()\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n            for alias in node.names:\n                imports.add(alias.name)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n            if node.module:\n                imports.add(node.module)\n                for alias in node.names:\n                    imports.add(f\"{node.module}.{alias.name}\")\n    return imports\n\n\ndef analyze_orphan_modules(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect Python modules in provider directories with zero inbound imports.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.2):\n    1. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n       the provider dir imports it\n    3. If zero importers, emit orphan_module finding\n    4. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n    \"\"\"\n    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n    if not provider_dirs:\n        return []\n\n    # Collect all Python files and parse them for imports\n    all_files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, [])\n    all_imports: set[str] = set()\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in all_files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    # Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n    for f, tree in trees.items():\n        is_in_provider = any(\n            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n        )\n        if not is_in_provider:\n            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n            # Apply exclude patterns\n            if any(fnmatch(py_file.name, pat) for pat in config.exclude_patterns):\n                continue\n\n            # Derive the module path components\n            try:\n                rel = py_file.relative_to(source_dir)\n            except ValueError:\n                continue\n\n            # Build possible import names\n            module_stem = py_file.stem\n            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n\n            # Check if any external file imports this module\n            is_imported = False\n            for imp in all_imports:\n                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n                    is_imported = True\n                    break\n\n            if not is_imported:\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n                        file_path=str(py_file),\n                        symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n                        line_number=1,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n                            f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"major\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-003: Registry Analysis (section 5.2.3) ---\n\n\ndef _matches_registry_pattern(\n    name: str, patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a variable name matches any registry detection pattern.\"\"\"\n    return any(p.match(name) for p in patterns)\n\n\ndef _resolve_name_in_scope(\n    name: str, tree: ast.Module, all_imports: set[str]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a name is resolvable: defined in module or importable.\"\"\"\n    # Check module-level definitions\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n                    return True\n\n    # Check if importable\n    if name in all_imports:\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_registries(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n\n        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n                continue\n\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n                    continue\n                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n                    continue\n\n                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n                    continue\n\n                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n                    if val_node is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Explicit None is allowed\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n                        val_node.value, str\n                    ):\n                        ref = val_node.value\n                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"string path '{ref}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Top-level entry point\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_wiring_analysis(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> WiringReport:\n    \"\"\"Run all three wiring analyzers and produce a WiringReport.\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        WiringReport aggregating findings from all analyzers.\n    \"\"\"\n    start = time.monotonic()\n\n    _, skipped = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files_analyzed = len(files)\n\n    unwired = analyze_unwired_callables(config, source_dir)\n    orphans = analyze_orphan_modules(config, source_dir)\n    registries = analyze_registries(config, source_dir)\n\n    duration = time.monotonic() - start\n\n    return WiringReport(\n        target_dir=str(source_dir),\n        files_analyzed=files_analyzed,\n        files_skipped=skipped,\n        unwired_callables=unwired,\n        orphan_modules=orphans,\n        unwired_registries=registries,\n        scan_duration_seconds=round(duration, 4),\n        rollout_mode=config.rollout_mode,\n    )\n```\n\n2. `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/audit/wiring_analyzer.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"AST-based file analyzer for ToolOrchestrator integration.\n\nProvides ast_analyze_file() as a drop-in replacement for the default\nline-based analyzer in ToolOrchestrator. Populates the `references`\nfield that the default analyzer leaves empty, enabling improved\ndependency graph, dead code, and profile analysis.\n\nThis module has zero imports from pipeline/* (NFR-007 compliance).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport ast\nimport logging\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.audit.tool_orchestrator import (\n    FileAnalysis,\n    compute_content_hash,\n)\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\ndef ast_analyze_file(file_path: str, content: str) -> FileAnalysis:\n    \"\"\"Parse a Python file using AST and return structured analysis.\n\n    Drop-in replacement for ToolOrchestrator's default analyzer. Extracts:\n    - imports: All import statements (import X, from X import Y)\n    - exports: Symbols listed in __all__, or top-level public definitions\n    - references: Cross-file name references (function calls, attribute access)\n\n    Handles SyntaxError gracefully per R2: returns empty FileAnalysis with\n    error metadata instead of raising.\n\n    Args:\n        file_path: Path to the file being analyzed.\n        content: Source code content of the file.\n\n    Returns:\n        FileAnalysis with populated imports, exports, and references.\n    \"\"\"\n    content_hash = compute_content_hash(content)\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n\n    try:\n        tree = ast.parse(content, filename=file_path)\n    except SyntaxError as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"SyntaxError in %s: %s — returning empty analysis\", file_path, exc)\n        return FileAnalysis(\n            file_path=file_path,\n            content_hash=content_hash,\n            imports=[],\n            exports=[],\n            references=[],\n            metadata={\n                \"line_count\": len(lines),\n                \"size_bytes\": len(content),\n                \"parse_error\": str(exc),\n            },\n        )\n\n    imports = _extract_imports(tree)\n    exports = _extract_exports(tree)\n    references = _extract_references(tree)\n\n    return FileAnalysis(\n        file_path=file_path,\n        content_hash=content_hash,\n        imports=imports,\n        exports=exports,\n        references=references,\n        metadata={\n            \"line_count\": len(lines),\n            \"size_bytes\": len(content),\n        },\n    )\n\n\ndef _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract import statements from AST.\"\"\"\n    imports: list[str] = []\n\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n            for alias in node.names:\n                imports.append(f\"import {alias.name}\")\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n            module = node.module or \"\"\n            for alias in node.names:\n                imports.append(f\"from {module} import {alias.name}\")\n\n    return imports\n\n\ndef _extract_exports(tree: ast.Module) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract exported symbols from AST.\n\n    Looks for __all__ assignment first. If absent, collects top-level\n    public function and class definitions.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Check for __all__\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == \"__all__\":\n                    if isinstance(node.value, (ast.List, ast.Tuple)):\n                        return [\n                            elt.value\n                            for elt in node.value.elts\n                            if isinstance(elt, ast.Constant) and isinstance(elt.value, str)\n                        ]\n\n    # Fallback: top-level public definitions\n    exports: list[str] = []\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if not node.name.startswith(\"_\"):\n                exports.append(node.name)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if not node.name.startswith(\"_\"):\n                exports.append(node.name)\n\n    return exports\n\n\ndef _extract_references(tree: ast.Module) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract cross-file name references from AST.\n\n    Collects:\n    - Function/method call targets\n    - Attribute access chains (module.function patterns)\n    - Name references in assignments and expressions\n    \"\"\"\n    references: set[str] = set()\n\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n            ref = _call_target_name(node)\n            if ref:\n                references.add(ref)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Attribute):\n            ref = _attribute_chain(node)\n            if ref:\n                references.add(ref)\n\n    return sorted(references)\n\n\ndef _call_target_name(call: ast.Call) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Extract the target name from a Call node.\"\"\"\n    func = call.func\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Name):\n        return func.id\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute):\n        return _attribute_chain(func)\n    return None\n\n\ndef _attribute_chain(node: ast.Attribute) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Build a dotted name from an Attribute chain (e.g., foo.bar.baz).\"\"\"\n    parts: list[str] = [node.attr]\n    current = node.value\n\n    while isinstance(current, ast.Attribute):\n        parts.append(current.attr)\n        current = current.value\n\n    if isinstance(current, ast.Name):\n        parts.append(current.id)\n        return \".\".join(reversed(parts))\n\n    return None\n```\n\n3. `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/audit/wiring_config.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Wiring analysis configuration and whitelist loading.\n\nProvides WiringConfig for controlling wiring analysis behavior including\nprovider directory conventions, exclude patterns, registry detection patterns,\nand whitelist-based suppression. Whitelist strictness varies by rollout_mode\nper OQ-3 decision (D-0001).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport logging\nimport re\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Literal\n\nimport yaml\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n# Default regex patterns for dispatch registry detection (section 4.2.1).\n# Matches module-level dict assignments named like STEP_REGISTRY, FOO_DISPATCH, etc.\nDEFAULT_REGISTRY_PATTERNS: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...] = (\n    re.compile(r\"^[A-Z_]*REGISTRY$\"),\n    re.compile(r\"^[A-Z_]*DISPATCH$\"),\n    re.compile(r\"^[A-Z_]*HANDLERS$\"),\n    re.compile(r\"^[A-Z_]*ROUTER$\"),\n    re.compile(r\"^[A-Z_]*BUILDERS$\"),\n    re.compile(r\"^PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS$\"),\n)\n\n\nclass WiringConfigError(Exception):\n    \"\"\"Raised for invalid whitelist or config in non-shadow rollout modes.\"\"\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass WhitelistEntry:\n    \"\"\"A single suppression entry from wiring_whitelist.yaml.\"\"\"\n\n    symbol: str\n    reason: str\n    finding_type: str = \"unwired_callable\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass WiringConfig:\n    \"\"\"Configuration for the wiring analysis engine.\n\n    Fields:\n        provider_dir_names: Directory basenames treated as provider directories\n            for orphan module detection (section 5.2.2).\n        exclude_patterns: Glob patterns for files excluded from analysis.\n            Excluded files increment files_skipped per OQ-2.\n        registry_patterns: Compiled regex patterns for identifying dispatch\n            registry variables in source files (section 5.2.3).\n        whitelist_path: Path to wiring_whitelist.yaml for suppression entries.\n            None means no whitelist suppression.\n        rollout_mode: Controls strictness of whitelist validation and\n            blocking semantics per OQ-3/OQ-6.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    provider_dir_names: frozenset[str] = frozenset(\n        {\"steps\", \"handlers\", \"validators\", \"checks\"}\n    )\n    exclude_patterns: list[str] = field(\n        default_factory=lambda: [\"test_*.py\", \"conftest.py\", \"__init__.py\"]\n    )\n    registry_patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...] = DEFAULT_REGISTRY_PATTERNS\n    whitelist_path: Path | None = None\n    rollout_mode: Literal[\"shadow\", \"soft\", \"full\"] = \"shadow\"\n\n\ndef load_whitelist(\n    path: Path | None,\n    rollout_mode: Literal[\"shadow\", \"soft\", \"full\"] = \"shadow\",\n) -> list[WhitelistEntry]:\n    \"\"\"Load suppression entries from a wiring whitelist YAML file.\n\n    Args:\n        path: Path to whitelist YAML. Returns empty list if None or nonexistent.\n        rollout_mode: Controls error handling for malformed entries.\n            - shadow: warn and skip malformed entries (OQ-3)\n            - soft/full: raise WiringConfigError on malformed entries\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WhitelistEntry instances for suppression matching.\n    \"\"\"\n    if path is None or not path.exists():\n        return []\n\n    try:\n        raw = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\"))\n    except yaml.YAMLError as exc:\n        if rollout_mode == \"shadow\":\n            logger.warning(\"Malformed whitelist YAML at %s: %s\", path, exc)\n            return []\n        raise WiringConfigError(\n            f\"Malformed whitelist YAML at {path}: {exc}\"\n        ) from exc\n\n    if not isinstance(raw, dict):\n        if rollout_mode == \"shadow\":\n            logger.warning(\"Whitelist at %s is not a mapping, skipping\", path)\n            return []\n        raise WiringConfigError(f\"Whitelist at {path} is not a mapping\")\n\n    entries: list[WhitelistEntry] = []\n\n    for section_key in (\"unwired_callables\", \"orphan_modules\", \"unwired_registries\"):\n        section = raw.get(section_key, [])\n        if not isinstance(section, list):\n            if rollout_mode == \"shadow\":\n                logger.warning(\n                    \"Whitelist section '%s' is not a list, skipping\", section_key\n                )\n                continue\n            raise WiringConfigError(\n                f\"Whitelist section '{section_key}' is not a list\"\n            )\n\n        # Map section keys to finding_type values\n        finding_type_map = {\n            \"unwired_callables\": \"unwired_callable\",\n            \"orphan_modules\": \"orphan_module\",\n            \"unwired_registries\": \"unwired_registry\",\n        }\n        finding_type = finding_type_map[section_key]\n\n        for item in section:\n            if not isinstance(item, dict) or \"symbol\" not in item:\n                if rollout_mode == \"shadow\":\n                    logger.warning(\n                        \"Malformed whitelist entry in '%s': %r, skipping\",\n                        section_key,\n                        item,\n                    )\n                    continue\n                raise WiringConfigError(\n                    f\"Malformed whitelist entry in '{section_key}': {item!r}\"\n                )\n\n            entries.append(\n                WhitelistEntry(\n                    symbol=item[\"symbol\"],\n                    reason=item.get(\"reason\", \"\"),\n                    finding_type=finding_type,\n                )\n            )\n\n    return entries\n```\n\n4.        skipped += 1\n            continue\n        included.append(py_file)\n\n    return included, skipped\n\n\ndef _safe_parse(file_path: Path) -> ast.Module | None:\n    \"\"\"Parse a Python file, returning None on SyntaxError (R2 mitigation).\"\"\"\n    try:\n        source = file_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        return ast.parse(source, filename=str(file_path))\n    except SyntaxError as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"SyntaxError parsing %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n    except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"Cannot read %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n\n\ndef _apply_whitelist(\n    findings: list[WiringFinding],\n    whitelist: list[WhitelistEntry],\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Mark findings as suppressed if they match a whitelist entry.\"\"\"\n    suppressed_symbols = {\n        (e.symbol, e.finding_type) for e in whitelist\n    }\n    for finding in findings:\n        if (finding.symbol_name, finding.finding_type) in suppressed_symbols:\n            finding.suppressed = True\n            finding.severity = \"info\"\n    return findings\n\n\n# --- G-001: Unwired Callable Analysis (section 5.2.1) ---\n\n\ndef _extract_injectable_params(\n    tree: ast.Module, file_path: str\n) -> list[tuple[str, str, int]]:\n    \"\"\"Extract Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n\n    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n    \"\"\"\n    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if not isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            continue\n\n        for item in node.body:\n            if not isinstance(item, ast.FunctionDef) or item.name != \"__init__\":\n                continue\n\n            for arg in item.args.args:\n                if arg.arg == \"self\":\n                    continue\n                annotation = arg.annotation\n                if annotation is None:\n                    continue\n\n                # Check for Optional[Callable] or Callable | None\n                if _is_optional_callable(annotation):\n                    # Verify default is None\n                    if _has_none_default(item, arg):\n                        symbol = f\"{node.name}.{arg.arg}\"\n                        injectables.append(\n                            (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n                        )\n\n    return injectables\n\n\ndef _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n            slice_val = annotation.slice\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                return True\n            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n                slice_val = annotation.slice\n                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n\n    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n            return True\n        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n            return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n    args = func_def.args\n    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n    all_args = args.args\n    defaults = args.defaults\n\n    if not defaults:\n        return False\n\n    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n        if arg is target_arg:\n            default_idx = i - offset\n            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n                default = defaults[default_idx]\n                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n    return False\n\n\ndef _find_wiring_call_sites(\n    param_name: str,\n    class_name: str,\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n    for tree in trees.values():\n        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                # Check keyword arguments\n                for kw in node.keywords:\n                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n                            return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n    func = call.func\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n        return True\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_unwired_callables(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n    1. Parse all Python files, extract Optional[Callable] constructor params\n    2. For each injectable, search all files for keyword call sites\n    3. If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n    4. Apply whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_callable\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        injectables = _extract_injectable_params(tree, str(file_path))\n        for symbol, param_name, lineno in injectables:\n            class_name = symbol.split(\".\")[0]\n            if not _find_wiring_call_sites(param_name, class_name, trees):\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"unwired_callable\",\n                        file_path=str(file_path),\n                        symbol_name=symbol,\n                        line_number=lineno,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Parameter '{param_name}' typed Optional[Callable] \"\n                            f\"with default None is never wired by any call site\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"critical\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-002: Orphan Module Analysis (section 5.2.2) ---\n\n\ndef _find_provider_dirs(source_dir: Path, provider_names: frozenset[str]) -> list[Path]:\n    \"\"\"Find directories matching provider_dir_names convention.\"\"\"\n    providers: list[Path] = []\n    for d in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*\")):\n        if d.is_dir() and d.name in provider_names:\n            providers.append(d)\n    return providers\n\n\ndef _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> set[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract all imported module/symbol names from an AST.\"\"\"\n    imports: set[str] = set()\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n            for alias in node.names:\n                imports.add(alias.name)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n            if node.module:\n                imports.add(node.module)\n                for alias in node.names:\n                    imports.add(f\"{node.module}.{alias.name}\")\n    return imports\n\n\ndef analyze_orphan_modules(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect Python modules in provider directories with zero inbound imports.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.2):\n    1. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n       the provider dir imports it\n    3. If zero importers, emit orphan_module finding\n    4. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n    \"\"\"\n    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n    if not provider_dirs:\n        return []\n\n    # Collect all Python files and parse them for imports\n    all_files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, [])\n    all_imports: set[str] = set()\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in all_files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    # Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n    for f, tree in trees.items():\n        is_in_provider = any(\n            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n        )\n        if not is_in_provider:\n            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n            # Apply exclude patterns\n            if any(fnmatch(py_file.name, pat) for pat in config.exclude_patterns):\n                continue\n\n            # Derive the module path components\n            try:\n                rel = py_file.relative_to(source_dir)\n            except ValueError:\n                continue\n\n            # Build possible import names\n            module_stem = py_file.stem\n            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n\n            # Check if any external file imports this module\n            is_imported = False\n            for imp in all_imports:\n                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n                    is_imported = True\n                    break\n\n            if not is_imported:\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n                        file_path=str(py_file),\n                        symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n                        line_number=1,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n                            f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"major\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-003: Registry Analysis (section 5.2.3) ---\n\n\ndef _matches_registry_pattern(\n    name: str, patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a variable name matches any registry detection pattern.\"\"\"\n    return any(p.match(name) for p in patterns)\n\n\ndef _resolve_name_in_scope(\n    name: str, tree: ast.Module, all_imports: set[str]\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a name is resolvable: defined in module or importable.\"\"\"\n    # Check module-level definitions\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n                    return True\n\n    # Check if importable\n    if name in all_imports:\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_registries(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n\n        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n                continue\n\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n                    continue\n                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n                    continue\n\n                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n                    continue\n\n                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n                    if val_node is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Explicit None is allowed\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n                        continue\n\n                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n                        val_node.value, str\n                    ):\n                        ref = val_node.value\n                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n                        ):\n                            key_repr = (\n                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n                            )\n                            findings.append(\n                                WiringFinding(\n                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n                                    detail=(\n                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n                                        f\"string path '{ref}'\"\n                                    ),\n                                    severity=\"critical\",\n                                )\n                            )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Top-level entry point\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef run_wiring_analysis(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> WiringReport:\n    \"\"\"Run all three wiring analyzers and produce a WiringReport.\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        WiringReport aggregating findings from all analyzers.\n    \"\"\"\n    start = time.monotonic()\n\n    _, skipped = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    files_analyzed = len(files)\n\n    unwired = analyze_unwired_callables(config, source_dir)\n    orphans = analyze_orphan_modules(config, source_dir)\n    registries = analyze_registries(config, source_dir)\n\n    duration = time.monotonic() - start\n\n    return WiringReport(\n        target_dir=str(source_dir),\n        files_analyzed=files_analyzed,\n        files_skipped=skipped,\n        unwired_callables=unwired,\n        orphan_modules=orphans,\n        unwired_registries=registries,\n        scan_duration_seconds=round(duration, 4),\n        rollout_mode=config.rollout_mode,\n    )\n```\n\n2. `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/audit/wiring_analyzer.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"AST-based file analyzer for ToolOrchestrator integration.\n\nProvides ast_analyze_file() as a drop-in replacement for the default\nline-based analyzer in ToolOrchestrator. Populates the `references`\nfield that the default analyzer leaves empty, enabling improved\ndependency graph, dead code, and profile analysis.\n\nThis module has zero imports from pipeline/* (NFR-007 compliance).\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport ast\nimport logging\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.audit.tool_orchestrator import (\n    FileAnalysis,\n    compute_content_hash,\n)\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\ndef ast_analyze_file(file_path: str, content: str) -> FileAnalysis:\n    \"\"\"Parse a Python file using AST and return structured analysis.\n\n    Drop-in replacement for ToolOrchestrator's default analyzer. Extracts:\n    - imports: All import statements (import X, from X import Y)\n    - exports: Symbols listed in __all__, or top-level public definitions\n    - references: Cross-file name references (function calls, attribute access)\n\n    Handles SyntaxError gracefully per R2: returns empty FileAnalysis with\n    error metadata instead of raising.\n\n    Args:\n        file_path: Path to the file being analyzed.\n        content: Source code content of the file.\n\n    Returns:\n        FileAnalysis with populated imports, exports, and references.\n    \"\"\"\n    content_hash = in %s: %s — returning empty analysis\", file_path, exc)\n        return FileAnalysis(\n            file_path=file_path,\n            content_hash=content_hash,\n            imports=[],\n            exports=[],\n            references=[],\n            metadata={\n                \"line_count\": len(lines),\n                \"size_bytes\": len(content),\n                \"parse_error\": str(exc),\n            },\n        )\n\n    imports = _extract_imports(tree)\n    exports = _extract_exports(tree)\n    references = _extract_references(tree)\n\n    return FileAnalysis(\n        file_path=file_path,\n        content_hash=content_hash,\n        imports=imports,\n        exports=exports,\n        references=references,\n        metadata={\n            \"line_count\": len(lines),\n            \"size_bytes\": len(content),\n        },\n    )\n\n\ndef _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract import statements from AST.\"\"\"\n    imports: elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n            module = node.module or \"\"\n            for alias in node.names:\n                imports.append(f\"from {module} import {alias.name}\")\n\n    return imports\n\n\ndef _extract_exports(tree: ast.Module) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract exported symbols from AST.\n\n    Looks for __all__ assignment first. If absent, collects top-level\n    public function and class definitions.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Check for __all__\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == \"__all__\":\n                    if isinstance(node.value, (ast.List, ast.Tuple)):\n                        return [\n                            elt.value\n                            for elt in node.value.elts\n                            if isinstance(elt, ast.Constant) and isinstance(elt.value, str)\n                        ]\n\n    # Fallback: top-level public definitions\n    exports: list[str] = []\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if not node.name.startswith(\"_\"):\n                exports.append(node.name)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if not node.name.startswith(\"_\"):\n                exports.append(node.name)\n\n    return exports\n\n\ndef _extract_references(tree: ast.Module) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract cross-file name references from AST.\n\n    Collects:\n    - Function/method call targets\n    - Attribute access chains (module.function patterns)\n    - Name references in assignments and expressions\n    \"\"\"\n    references: set[str] = set()\n\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n            ref = _call_target_name(node)\n            if ref:\n                references.add(ref)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Attribute):\n            ref = _attribute_chain(node)\n            if ref:\n                references.add(ref)\n\n    return sorted(references)\n\n\ndef _call_target_name(call: ast.Call) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Extract the target name from a Call node.\"\"\"\n    func = call.func\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Name):\n        return func.id\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute):\n        return _attribute_chain(func)\n    return None\n\n\ndef _attribute_chain(node: ast.Attribute) -> str | None:\n    \"\"\"Build a dotted name from an Attribute chain (e.g., foo.bar.baz).\"\"\"\n    parts: list[str] = [node.attr]\n    current = node.value\n\n    while isinstance(current, ast.Attribute):\n        parts.append(current.attr)\n        current = current.value\n\n    if isinstance(current, ast.Name):\n        parts.append(current.id)\n        return \".\".join(reversed(parts))\n\n    return None\n```\n\n3. `/config/workspace/IronClaude/src/superclaude/cli/audit/wiring_config.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Wiring analysis configuration and whitelist loading.\n\nProvides WiringConfig for controlling wiring analysis behavior including\nprovider directory conventions, exclude patterns, registry detection patterns,\nand whitelist-based suppression.
