16→from fnmatch import fnmatch\n    17→from pathlib import Path\n    18→from typing import Literal\n    19→\n    20→from superclaude.cli.audit.wiring_config import (\n    21→    WiringConfig,\n    22→    WhitelistEntry,\n    23→    load_whitelist,\n    24→)\n    25→\n    26→logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n    27→\n    28→\n    29→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    30→# Data models (section 5.1)\n    31→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    32→\n    33→\n    34→@dataclass\n    35→class WiringFinding:\n    36→    \"\"\"A single wiring integrity finding.\n    37→\n    38→    Attributes:\n    39→        finding_type: Category of the finding.\n    40→        file_path: Path to the file where the issue was detected.\n    41→        symbol_name: Fully-qualified symbol name involved.\n    42→        line_number: Line number in the source file.\n    43→        detail: Human-readable evidence description.\n    44→        severity: Impact severity for gate evaluation.\n    45→        suppressed: True if matched by a whitelist entry.\n    46→    \"\"\"\n    47→\n    48→    finding_type: Literal[\"unwired_callable\", \"orphan_module\", \"unwired_registry\"]\n    49→    file_path: str\n    50→    symbol_name: str\n    51→    line_number: int\n    52→    detail: str\n    53→    severity: Literal[\"critical\", \"major\", \"info\"] = \"critical\"\n    54→    suppressed: bool = False\n    55→\n    56→\n    57→@dataclass\n    58→class WiringReport:\n    59→    \"\"\"Aggregated wiring analysis report.\n    60→\n    61→    Single-source-of-truth invariant: category sums == severity sums == total.\n    62→    Blocking count is derived from rollout_mode per OQ-6.\n    63→\n    64→    Attributes:\n    65→        target_dir: Root directory that was analyzed.\n    66→        files_analyzed: Number of Python files successfully parsed.\n    67→        files_skipped: Number of files excluded or unparseable (OQ-2).\n    68→        unwired_callables: Findings from unwired callable analysis (G-001).\n    69→        orphan_modules: Findings from orphan module analysis (G-002).\n    70→        unwired_registries: Findings from registry analysis (G-003).\n    71→        scan_duration_seconds: Wall-clock time of analysis run.\n    72→        rollout_mode: Active rollout mode for blocking semantics.\n    73→    \"\"\"\n    74→\n    75→    target_dir: str = \"\"\n    76→    files_analyzed: int = 0\n    77→    files_skipped: int = 0\n    78→    unwired_callables: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    79→    orphan_modules: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    80→    unwired_registries: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    81→    scan_duration_seconds: float = 0.0\n    82→    rollout_mode: str = \"shadow\"\n    83→\n    84→    @property\n    85→    def all_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    86→        \"\"\"All findings across all categories.\"\"\"\n    87→        return self.unwired_callables + self.orphan_modules + self.unwired_registries\n    88→\n    89→    @property\n    90→    def total_findings(self) -> int:\n    91→        \"\"\"Total finding count (category sum invariant).\"\"\"\n    92→        return len(self.all_findings)\n    93→\n    94→    @property\n    95→    def unsuppressed_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    96→        \"\"\"Findings not suppressed by whitelist.\"\"\"\n    97→        return [f for f in self.all_findings if not f.suppressed]\n    98→\n    99→    @property\n   100→    def clean(self) -> bool:\n   101→        \"\"\"True if zero unsuppressed findings regardless of rollout mode.\"\"\"\n   102→        return len(self.unsuppressed_findings) == 0\n   103→\n   104→    def blocking_count(self, mode: str | None = None) -> int:\n   105→        \"\"\"Count of findings that block the gate for the given rollout mode.\n   106→\n   107→        Args:\n   108→            mode: Override rollout mode. Uses self.rollout_mode if None.\n   109→\n   110→        Returns:\n   111→            Number of blocking findings per OQ-6:\n   112→            - shadow: 0 (never blocks)\n   113→            - soft: critical unsuppressed only\n   114→            - full: critical + major unsuppressed\n   115→        \"\"\"\n   116→        effective_mode = mode or self.rollout_mode\n   117→        unsuppressed = self.unsuppressed_findings\n   118→\n   119→        if effective_mode == \"shadow\":\n   120→            return 0\n   121→        elif effective_mode == \"soft\":\n   122→            return sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n   123→        else:  # full\n   124→            return sum(\n   125→                1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity in (\"critical\", \"major\")\n   126→            )\n   127→\n   128→\n   129→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   130→# Analyzers (sections 5.2.1, 5.2.2, 5.2.3)\n   131→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   132→\n   133→\n   134→def _collect_python_files(\n   135→    source_dir: Path,\n   136→    exclude_patterns: list[str],\n   137→) -> tuple[list[Path], int]:\n   138→    \"\"\"Collect Python files from source_dir, applying exclude patterns.\n   139→\n   140→    Returns:\n   141→        Tuple of (included files, skipped count).\n   142→    \"\"\"\n   143→    included: list[Path] = []\n   144→    skipped = 0\n   145→\n   146→    for py_file in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*.py\")):\n   147→        name = py_file.name\n   148→        if any(fnmatch(name, pat) for pat in exclude_patterns):\n   149→            skipped += 1\n   150→            continue\n   151→        included.append(py_file)\n   152→\n   153→    return included, skipped\n   154→\n   155→\n   156→def _safe_parse(file_path: Path) -> ast.Module | None:\n   157→    \"\"\"Parse a Python file, returning None on SyntaxError (R2 mitigation).\"\"\"\n   158→    try:\n   159→        source = file_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   160→        return ast.parse(source, filename=str(file_path))\n   161→    except SyntaxError as exc:\n   162→        logger.warning(\"SyntaxError parsing %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n   163→        return None\n   164→    except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as exc:\n   165→        logger.warning(\"Cannot read %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n   166→        return None\n   167→\n   168→\n   169→def _apply_whitelist(\n   170→    findings: list[WiringFinding],\n   171→    whitelist: list[WhitelistEntry],\n   172→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   173→    \"\"\"Mark findings as suppressed if they match a whitelist entry.\"\"\"\n   174→    suppressed_symbols = {\n   175→        (e.symbol, e.finding_type) for e in whitelist\n   176→    }\n   177→    for finding in findings:\n   178→        if (finding.symbol_name, finding.finding_type) in suppressed_symbols:\n   179→            finding.suppressed = True\n   180→            finding.severity = \"info\"\n   181→    return findings\n   182→\n   183→\n   184→# --- G-001: Unwired Callable Analysis (section 5.2.1) ---\n   185→\n   186→\n   187→def _extract_injectable_params(\n   188→    tree: ast.Module, file_path: str\n   189→) -> list[tuple[str, str, int]]:\n   190→    \"\"\"Extract Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n   191→\n   192→    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n   193→    \"\"\"\n   194→    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n   195→\n   196→    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   197→        if not isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n   198→            continue\n   199→\n   200→        for item in node.body:\n   201→            if not isinstance(item, ast.FunctionDef) or item.name != \"__init__\":\n   202→                continue\n   203→\n   204→            for arg in item.args.args:\n   205→                if arg.arg == \"self\":\n   206→                    continue\n   207→                annotation = arg.annotation\n   208→                if annotation is None:\n   209→                    continue\n   210→\n   211→                # Check for Optional[Callable] or Callable | None\n   212→                if _is_optional_callable(annotation):\n   213→                    # Verify default is None\n   214→                    if _has_none_default(item, arg):\n   215→                        symbol = f\"{node.name}.{arg.arg}\"\n   216→                        injectables.append(\n   217→                            (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n   218→                        )\n   219→\n   220→    return injectables\n   221→\n   222→\n   223→def _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n   224→    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n   225→    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n   226→    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n   227→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n   228→            slice_val = annotation.slice\n   229→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   230→                return True\n   231→            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n   232→            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n   233→                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n   234→                    return True\n   235→        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n   236→        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n   237→            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n   238→                slice_val = annotation.slice\n   239→                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n   240→                    return True\n   241→\n   242→    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n   243→    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n   244→        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n   245→        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n   246→                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n   247→            return True\n   248→        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n   249→                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n   250→            return True\n   251→\n   252→    return False\n   253→\n   254→\n   255→def _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n   256→    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n   257→    args = func_def.args\n   258→    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n   259→    all_args = args.args\n   260→    defaults = args.defaults\n   261→\n   262→    if not defaults:\n   263→        return False\n   264→\n   265→    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n   266→    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n   267→    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n   268→        if arg is target_arg:\n   269→            default_idx = i - offset\n   270→            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n   271→                default = defaults[default_idx]\n   272→                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n   273→    return False\n   274→\n   275→\n   276→def _find_wiring_call_sites(\n   277→    param_name: str,\n   278→    class_name: str,\n   279→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n   280→) -> bool:\n   281→    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n   282→    for tree in trees.values():\n   283→        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   284→            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n   285→                # Check keyword arguments\n   286→                for kw in node.keywords:\n   287→                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n   288→                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n   289→                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n   290→                            return True\n   291→    return False\n   292→\n   293→\n   294→def _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n   295→    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n   296→    func = call.func\n   297→    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n   298→        return True\n   299→    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n   300→        return True\n   301→    return False\n   302→\n   303→\n   304→def analyze_unwired_callables(\n   305→    config: WiringConfig,\n   306→    source_dir: Path,\n   307→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   308→    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n   309→\n   310→    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n   311→    1. Parse all Python files, extract Optional[Callable] constructor params\n   312→    2. For each injectable, search all files for keyword call sites\n   313→    3. If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n   314→    4. Apply whitelist suppression\n   315→\n   316→    Args:\n   317→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   318→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   319→\n   320→    Returns:\n   321→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_callable\".\n   322→    \"\"\"\n   323→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   324→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   325→\n   326→    for f in files:\n   327→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   328→        if tree is not None:\n   329→            trees[f] = tree\n   330→\n   331→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   332→\n   333→    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n   334→        injectables = _extract_injectable_params(tree, str(file_path))\n   335→        for symbol, param_name, lineno in injectables:\n   336→            class_name = symbol.split(\".\")[0]\n   337→            if not _find_wiring_call_sites(param_name, class_name, trees):\n   338→                findings.append(\n   339→                    WiringFinding(\n   340→                        finding_type=\"unwired_callable\",\n   341→                        file_path=str(file_path),\n   342→                        symbol_name=symbol,\n   343→                        line_number=lineno,\n   344→                        detail=(\n   345→                            f\"Parameter '{param_name}' typed Optional[Callable] \"\n   346→                            f\"with default None is never wired by any call site\"\n   347→                        ),\n   348→                        severity=\"critical\",\n   349→                    )\n   350→                )\n   351→\n   352→    # Apply whitelist\n   353→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   354→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   355→\n   356→\n   357→# --- G-002: Orphan Module Analysis (section 5.2.2) ---\n   358→\n   359→\n   360→def _find_provider_dirs(source_dir: Path, provider_names: frozenset[str]) -> list[Path]:\n   361→    \"\"\"Find directories matching provider_dir_names convention.\"\"\"\n   362→    providers: list[Path] = []\n   363→    for d in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*\")):\n   364→        if d.is_dir() and d.name in provider_names:\n   365→            providers.append(d)\n   366→    return providers\n   367→\n   368→\n   369→def _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> set[str]:\n   370→    \"\"\"Extract all imported module/symbol names from an AST.\"\"\"\n   371→    imports: set[str] = set()\n   372→    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n   373→        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n   374→            for alias in node.names:\n   375→                imports.add(alias.name)\n   376→        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n   377→            if node.module:\n   378→                imports.add(node.module)\n   379→                for alias in node.names:\n   380→                    imports.add(f\"{node.module}.{alias.name}\")\n   381→    return imports\n   382→\n   383→\n   384→def analyze_orphan_modules(\n   385→    config: WiringConfig,\n   386→    source_dir: Path,\n   387→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   388→    \"\"\"Detect Python modules in provider directories with zero inbound imports.\n   389→\n   390→    Algorithm (section 5.2.2):\n   391→    1. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n   392→    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n   393→       the provider dir imports it\n   394→    3. If zero importers, emit orphan_module finding\n   395→    4. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n   396→\n   397→    Args:\n   398→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   399→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   400→\n   401→    Returns:\n   402→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n   403→    \"\"\"\n   404→    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n   405→    if not provider_dirs:\n   406→        return []\n   407→\n   408→    # Collect all Python files and parse them for imports\n   409→    all_files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, [])\n   410→    all_imports: set[str] = set()\n   411→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   412→\n   413→    for f in all_files:\n   414→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   415→        if tree is not None:\n   416→            trees[f] = tree\n   417→\n   418→    # Gather imports from files OUTSIDE provider directories\n   419→    for f, tree in trees.items():\n   420→        is_in_provider = any(\n   421→            f.resolve().is_relative_to(pd.resolve()) for pd in provider_dirs\n   422→        )\n   423→        if not is_in_provider:\n   424→            all_imports.update(_extract_imports(tree))\n   425→\n   426→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   427→\n   428→    for provider_dir in provider_dirs:\n   429→        for py_file in sorted(provider_dir.glob(\"*.py\")):\n   430→            # Apply exclude patterns\n   431→            if any(fnmatch(py_file.name, pat) for pat in config.exclude_patterns):\n   432→                continue\n   433→\n   434→            # Derive the module path components\n   435→            try:\n   436→                rel = py_file.relative_to(source_dir)\n   437→            except ValueError:\n   438→                continue\n   439→\n   440→            # Build possible import names\n   441→            module_stem = py_file.stem\n   442→            module_dotpath = str(rel.with_suffix(\"\")).replace(\"/\", \".\").replace(\"\\\\\", \".\")\n   443→\n   444→            # Check if any external file imports this module\n   445→            is_imported = False\n   446→            for imp in all_imports:\n   447→                if module_dotpath in imp or module_stem in imp:\n   448→                    is_imported = True\n   449→                    break\n   450→\n   451→            if not is_imported:\n   452→                findings.append(\n   453→                    WiringFinding(\n   454→                        finding_type=\"orphan_module\",\n   455→                        file_path=str(py_file),\n   456→                        symbol_name=module_dotpath,\n   457→                        line_number=1,\n   458→                        detail=(\n   459→                            f\"Module '{module_dotpath}' in provider directory \"\n   460→                            f\"'{provider_dir.name}' has zero inbound imports\"\n   461→                        ),\n   462→                        severity=\"major\",\n   463→                    )\n   464→                )\n   465→\n   466→    # Apply whitelist\n   467→    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n   468→    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n   469→\n   470→\n   471→# --- G-003: Registry Analysis (section 5.2.3) ---\n   472→\n   473→\n   474→def _matches_registry_pattern(\n   475→    name: str, patterns: tuple[re.Pattern[str], ...]\n   476→) -> bool:\n   477→    \"\"\"Check if a variable name matches any registry detection pattern.\"\"\"\n   478→    return any(p.match(name) for p in patterns)\n   479→\n   480→\n   481→def _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   482→    name: str, tree: ast.Module, all_imports: set[str]\n   483→) -> bool:\n   484→    \"\"\"Check if a name is resolvable: defined in module or importable.\"\"\"\n   485→    # Check module-level definitions\n   486→    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n   487→        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n   488→            if node.name == name:\n   489→                return True\n   490→        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n   491→            if node.name == name:\n   492→                return True\n   493→        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n   494→            for target in node.targets:\n   495→                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n   496→                    return True\n   497→\n   498→    # Check if importable\n   499→    if name in all_imports:\n   500→        return True\n   501→\n   502→    return False\n   503→\n   504→\n   505→def analyze_registries(\n   506→    config: WiringConfig,\n   507→    source_dir: Path,\n   508→) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n   509→    \"\"\"Detect broken dispatch registry entries referencing nonexistent callables.\n   510→\n   511→    Algorithm (section 5.2.3):\n   512→    1. Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n   513→    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n   514→    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n   515→\n   516→    Args:\n   517→        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n   518→        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n   519→\n   520→    Returns:\n   521→        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n   522→    \"\"\"\n   523→    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n   524→    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n   525→    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n   526→\n   527→    for f in files:\n   528→        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n   529→        if tree is not None:\n   530→            trees[f] = tree\n   531→            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n   532→\n   533→    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n   534→\n   535→    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n   536→        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n   537→\n   538→        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n   539→            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n   540→                continue\n   541→\n   542→            for target in node.targets:\n   543→                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n   544→                    continue\n   545→                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n   546→                    continue\n   547→\n   548→                # This is a registry assignment — check if value is a dict\n   549→                if not isinstance(node.value, ast.Dict):\n   550→                    continue\n   551→\n   552→                for key_node, val_node in zip(node.value.keys, node.value.values):\n   553→                    if val_node is None:\n   554→                        continue\n   555→\n   556→                    # Explicit None is allowed\n   557→                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and val_node.value is None:\n   558→                        continue\n   559→\n   560→                    # Name reference — must be resolvable\n   561→                    if isinstance(val_node, ast.Name):\n   562→                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   563→                            val_node.id, tree, file_imports\n   564→                        ):\n   565→                            key_repr = (\n   566→                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n   567→                                if isinstance(key_node, ast.Constant)\n   568→                                else \"<dynamic>\"\n   569→                            )\n   570→                            findings.append(\n   571→                                WiringFinding(\n   572→                                    finding_type=\"unwired_registry\",\n   573→                                    file_path=str(file_path),\n   574→                                    symbol_name=f\"{target.id}[{key_repr!r}]\",\n   575→                                    line_number=val_node.lineno,\n   576→                                    detail=(\n   577→                                        f\"Registry '{target.id}' entry \"\n   578→                                        f\"'{key_repr}' references unresolvable \"\n   579→                                        f\"callable '{val_node.id}'\"\n   580→                                    ),\n   581→                                    severity=\"critical\",\n   582→                                )\n   583→                            )\n   584→\n   585→                    # String reference — try to resolve as dotted path\n   586→                    elif isinstance(val_node, ast.Constant) and isinstance(\n   587→                        val_node.value, str\n   588→                    ):\n   589→                        ref = val_node.value\n   590→                        parts = ref.rsplit(\".\", 1)\n   591→                        func_name = parts[-1] if len(parts) > 1 else ref\n   592→                        if not _resolve_name_in_scope(\n   593→                            func_name, tree, file_imports\n   594→                        ):\n   595→                            key_repr = (\n   596→                                ast.literal_eval(key_node)\n   597→ Integer/boolean gate-evaluated fields are exempt.\n\n**Whitelist visibility**: `whitelist_entries_applied` is ALWAYS present. Zero if no whitelist configured.\n\n<!-- Source: Variant A, Section 7.3 — required report body sections (S-002) -->\n#### 5.4.1 Required Body Sections\n\nThe Markdown body of the wiring verification report MUST contain these 7 sections in order:\n\n1. **Summary** -- overall finding counts, scope analyzed, rollout mode\n2. **Unwired Optional Callable Injections** -- per-finding detail for `unwired_callable` type\n3. **Orphan Modules / Symbols** -- per-finding detail for `orphan_module` type\n4. **Unregistered Dispatch Entries** -- per-finding detail for `unwired_registry` type\n5. **Suppressions and Dynamic Retention** -- whitelist entries applied, audit evidence used\n6. **Recommended Remediation** -- actionable fix guidance per finding category\n7. **Evidence and Limitations** -- known FPR sources, alias limitations, analysis boundaries\n\nThis ensures human-readable reports have consistent structure across runs and are useful for both automated gate validation and manual review.\n\n<!-- Source: Invariant INV-001 / Refactor W-004 — _extract_frontmatter_values() helper -->\n### 5.5 Frontmatter Value Extraction\n\nAll semantic check functions share a private helper:\n\n```python\ndef _extract_frontmatter_values(content: str) -> dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract frontmatter key-value pairs from report content.\n\n    Uses the _FRONTMATTER_RE regex pattern (duplicated from\n    pipeline/gates.py:77 as a private constant to preserve\n    NFR-007 layering) to extract frontmatter key-value pairs.\n\n    Returns a dict mapping each key to its raw string value.\n    Each semantic check calls this helper once and casts values\n    as needed (int(), string comparison).\n    \"\"\"\n```\n\nThis helper lives in `audit/wiring_gate.py`, not in `pipeline/*`, preserving the layering constraint (NFR-007). Estimated: ~15 LOC.\n\n**Why not modify `_check_frontmatter()`**: That function is in `pipeline/gates.py` which must remain domain-agnostic. Adding a value-extraction return type would change its contract, violating the \"zero changes to pipeline/*\" constraint.\n\n### 5.6 Gate Definition\n\n```python\nWIRING_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\n        \"gate\",\n        \"target_dir\",\n        \"files_analyzed\",\n        \"rollout_mode\",\n        \"analysis_complete\",\n        \"unwired_callable_count\",\n        \"orphan_module_count\",\n        \"unwired_registry_count\",\n        \"critical_count\",\n        \"major_count\",\n        \"info_count\",\n        \"total_findings\",\n        \"blocking_findings\",\n        \"whitelist_entries_applied\",\n        \"files_skipped\",\n        \"audit_artifacts_used\",\n    ],\n    min_lines=10,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STRICT\",\n true\",\n        ),\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"recognized_rollout_mode\",\n            check_fn=_recognized_rollout_mode,\n            failure_message=\"rollout_mode must be shadow, name=\"severity_summary_consistent\",\n            check_fn=_severity_summary_consistent,\n            failure_message=(\n                \"critical_count + major_count + info_count must equal total_findings\"\n            ),\n        ),\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"zero_blocking_findings_for_mode\",\n            check_fn=_zero_blocking_findings_for_mode,\n            failure_message=\"blocking_findings must be 0 for gate pass at current rollout_mode\",\n        ),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n**Mode-aware enforcement** (key design decision):\n\nThe `_zero_blocking_findings_for_mode` check reads `rollout_mode` and `blocking_findings` from frontmatter:\n- **shadow**: always returns `True` (findings logged, never block)\n- **soft**: returns `True` if `blocking_findings == 0` (only critical block)\n- **full**: returns `True` if `blocking_findings == 0` (all findings block)\n\nThe `blocking_findings` field is computed by the emitter based on rollout mode:\n- shadow: `blocking_findings = 0` always\n- soft: `blocking_findings = critical_count`\n- full: `blocking_findings = critical_count + major_count`\n\nThis encodes rollout policy into the report artifact, keeping semantic checks as pure content validators per the `SemanticCheck` contract.\n\n### 5.7 Roadmap Pipeline Integration\n\n**5-step process** (per gate-system-deep-analysis ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Data models (section 5.1)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass WiringFinding:\n    \"\"\"A single wiring integrity finding.\n\n    Attributes:\n        finding_type: Category of the finding.\n        file_path: Path to the file where the issue was detected.\n        symbol_name: Fully-qualified symbol name involved.\n        line_number: Line number in the source file.\n        detail: Human-readable evidence description.\n        severity: Impact severity for gate evaluation.\n        suppressed: True if matched by a whitelist entry.\n Literal[\"critical\", \"major\", \"info\"] = \"critical\"\n    suppressed: bool = False\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass WiringReport:\n    \"\"\"Aggregated wiring analysis report.\n\n    Single-source-of-truth invariant: category sums == severity sums == total.\n    Blocking count is derived from rollout_mode per OQ-6.\n\n    Attributes:\n        target_dir: Root directory that was analyzed.\n        files_analyzed: Number of Python files successfully parsed.\n        files_skipped: Number of files excluded or unparseable (OQ-2).\n        unwired_callables: Findings from unwired callable analysis (G-001).\n        orphan_modules: Findings from orphan module analysis (G-002).\n        unwired_registries: Findings from registry analysis (G-003).\n        scan_duration_seconds: Wall-clock time of analysis run.\n        rollout_mode: Active rollout mode for blocking semantics.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    target_dir: str = \"\"\n    files_analyzed: int = 0\n    files_skipped: int = 0\n    unwired_callables: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    orphan_modules: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    unwired_registries: list[WiringFinding] = field(default_factory=list)\n    scan_duration_seconds: float = 0.0\n    rollout_mode: str = \"shadow\"\n\n    @property\n    def all_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n        \"\"\"All findings across all categories.\"\"\"\n        return self.unwired_callables + self.orphan_modules + self.unwired_registries\n\n    @property\n    def total_findings(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Total finding count (category sum invariant).\"\"\"\n        return len(self.all_findings)\n\n    @property\n    def unsuppressed_findings(self) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n        \"\"\"Findings not suppressed by whitelist.\"\"\"\n        return [f for f in self.all_findings if not f.suppressed]\n\n    @property\n    def clean(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"True if zero unsuppressed findings regardless of rollout mode.\"\"\"\n        return len(self.unsuppressed_findings) == 0\n\n    def blocking_count(self, mode: str | None = None) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Count of findings that block the gate for the given rollout mode.\n\n        Args:\n            mode: Override rollout mode. Uses self.rollout_mode if None.\n\n        Returns:\n            Number of blocking findings per OQ-6:\n            - shadow: 0 (never blocks)\n            - soft: critical unsuppressed only\n            - full: critical + major unsuppressed\n        \"\"\"\n        effective_mode = mode or self.rollout_mode\n        unsuppressed = self.unsuppressed_findings\n\n        if effective_mode == \"shadow\":\n            return 0\n        elif effective_mode == \"soft\":\n            return sum(1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity == \"critical\")\n        else:  # full\n            return sum(\n                1 for f in unsuppressed if f.severity in (\"critical\", \"major\")\n            )\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Analyzers (sections 5.2.1, 5.2.2, 5.2.3)\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\ndef _collect_python_files(\n    source_dir: Path,\n    exclude_patterns: list[str],\n) -> tuple[list[Path], int]:\n    \"\"\"Collect Python files from source_dir, applying exclude patterns.\n\n    Returns:\n        Tuple of (included files, skipped count).\n    \"\"\"\n    included: list[Path] = []\n    skipped = 0\n\n    for py_file in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*.py\")):\n        name = py_file.name\n        if any(fnmatch(name, pat) for pat in exclude_patterns):\n            skipped += 1\n            continue\n        included.append(py_file)\n\n    return included, skipped\n\n\ndef _safe_parse(file_path: Path) -> ast.Module | None:\n    \"\"\"Parse a Python file, returning None on SyntaxError (R2 mitigation).\"\"\"\n    try:\n        source = file_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        return ast.parse(source, filename=str(file_path))\n    except SyntaxError as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"SyntaxError parsing %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n    except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as exc:\n        logger.warning(\"Cannot read %s: %s — skipping\", file_path, exc)\n        return None\n\n\ndef _apply_whitelist(\n    findings: list[WiringFinding],\n    whitelist: list[WhitelistEntry],\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Mark findings as suppressed if they match a whitelist entry.\"\"\"\n    suppressed_symbols = {\n        (e.symbol, e.finding_type) for e in whitelist\n    }\n    for finding in findings:\n        if (finding.symbol_name, finding.finding_type) in suppressed_symbols:\n            finding.suppressed = True\n            finding.severity = \"info\"\n    return findings\n\n\n# --- G-001: Unwired Callable Analysis (section 5.2.1) ---\n\n\ndef _extract_injectable_params(\n    tree: ast.Module, file_path: str\n) -> list[tuple[str, str, int]]:\n    \"\"\"Extract Optional[Callable] constructor parameters.\n\n    Returns list of (class_name.param_name, param_name, line_number).\n    \"\"\"\n    injectables: list[tuple[str, str, int]] = []\n\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if not isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            continue\n\n        for item in node.body:\n            if not isinstance(item, ast.FunctionDef) or item.name != \"__init__\":\n                continue\n\n            for arg in item.args.args:\n                if arg.arg == \"self\":\n                    continue\n                annotation = arg.annotation\n                if annotation is None:\n                    continue\n\n                # Check for Optional[Callable] or Callable | None\n                if _is_optional_callable(annotation):\n                    # Verify default is None\n                    if _has_none_default(item, arg):\n                        symbol = f\"{node.name}.{arg.arg}\"\n                        injectables.append(\n                            (symbol, arg.arg, arg.lineno)\n                        )\n\n    return injectables\n\n\ndef _is_optional_callable(annotation: ast.expr) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if an annotation represents Optional[Callable] or Callable | None.\"\"\"\n    # Optional[Callable] -> Subscript(Name('Optional'), Name('Callable'))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.Subscript):\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.id == \"Optional\":\n            slice_val = annotation.slice\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                return True\n            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and slice_val.value.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n        # Also check Attribute form: typing.Optional\n        if isinstance(annotation.value, ast.Attribute):\n            if annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n                slice_val = annotation.slice\n                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return True\n\n    # Callable | None -> BinOp(Name('Callable'), BitOr, Constant(None))\n    if isinstance(annotation, ast.BinOp) and isinstance(annotation.op, ast.BitOr):\n        left, right = annotation.left, annotation.right\n        if (isinstance(left, ast.Name) and left.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(right, ast.Constant) and right.value is None):\n            return True\n        if (isinstance(right, ast.Name) and right.id == \"Callable\" and\n                isinstance(left, ast.Constant) and left.value is None):\n            return True\n\n    return False\n\n\ndef _has_none_default(func_def: ast.FunctionDef, target_arg: ast.arg) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if the given arg has a default value of None.\"\"\"\n    args = func_def.args\n    # defaults apply to the last N positional args\n    all_args = args.args\n    defaults = args.defaults\n\n    if not defaults:\n        return False\n\n    # Map defaults to args (right-aligned)\n    offset = len(all_args) - len(defaults)\n    for i, arg in enumerate(all_args):\n        if arg is target_arg:\n            default_idx = i - offset\n            if 0 <= default_idx < len(defaults):\n                default = defaults[default_idx]\n                return isinstance(default, ast.Constant) and default.value is None\n    return False\n\n\ndef _find_wiring_call_sites(\n    param_name: str,\n    class_name: str,\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module],\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Search for call sites that explicitly provide the parameter by keyword.\"\"\"\n    for tree in trees.values():\n        for node in ast.walk(tree):\n            if isinstance(node, ast.Call):\n                # Check keyword arguments\n                for kw in node.keywords:\n                    if kw.arg == param_name:\n                        # Verify it's calling the right class\n                        if _is_class_call(node, class_name):\n                            return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef _is_class_call(call: ast.Call, class_name: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if a Call node is calling the specified class.\"\"\"\n    func = call.func\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Name) and func.id == class_name:\n        return True\n    if isinstance(func, ast.Attribute) and func.attr == class_name:\n        return True\n    return False\n\n\ndef analyze_unwired_callables(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect injectable callables (Optional[Callable]) that are never wired.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.1):\n    1. Parse all Python files, extract Optional[Callable] constructor params\n    2. For each injectable, search all files for keyword call sites\n    3. If zero providers, emit unwired_callable finding\n    4. Apply whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_callable\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        injectables = _extract_injectable_params(tree, str(file_path))\n        for symbol, param_name, lineno in injectables:\n            class_name = symbol.split(\".\")[0]\n            if not _find_wiring_call_sites(param_name, class_name, trees):\n                findings.append(\n                    WiringFinding(\n                        finding_type=\"unwired_callable\",\n                        file_path=str(file_path),\n                        symbol_name=symbol,\n                        line_number=lineno,\n                        detail=(\n                            f\"Parameter '{param_name}' typed Optional[Callable] \"\n                            f\"with default None is never wired by any call site\"\n                        ),\n                        severity=\"critical\",\n                    )\n                )\n\n    # Apply whitelist\n    whitelist = load_whitelist(config.whitelist_path, config.rollout_mode)\n    return _apply_whitelist(findings, whitelist)\n\n\n# --- G-002: Orphan Module Analysis (section 5.2.2) ---\n\n\ndef _find_provider_dirs(source_dir: Path, provider_names: frozenset[str]) -> list[Path]:\n    \"\"\"Find directories matching provider_dir_names convention.\"\"\"\n    providers: list[Path] = []\n    for d in sorted(source_dir.rglob(\"*\")):\n        if d.is_dir() and d.name in provider_names:\n            providers.append(d)\n    return providers\n\n\ndef _extract_imports(tree: ast.Module) -> set[str]:\n    \"\"\"Extract all imported module/symbol names from an AST.\"\"\"\n    imports: set[str] = set()\n    for node in ast.walk(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, ast.Import):\n            for alias in node.names:\n                imports.add(alias.name)\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ImportFrom):\n            if node.module:\n                imports.add(node.module)\n                for alias in node.names:\n                    imports.add(f\"{node.module}.{alias.name}\")\n    return imports\n\n\ndef analyze_orphan_modules(\n    config: WiringConfig,\n    source_dir: Path,\n) -> list[WiringFinding]:\n    \"\"\"Detect Python modules in provider directories with zero inbound imports.\n\n    Algorithm (section 5.2.2):\n    1. Find provider directories by config.provider_dir_names convention\n    2. For each Python file in provider dirs, check if any file outside\n       the provider dir imports it\n    3. If zero importers, emit orphan_module finding\n    4. Apply exclude_patterns and whitelist suppression\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"orphan_module\".\n    \"\"\"\n    provider_dirs = _find_provider_dirs(source_dir, config.provider_dir_names)\n    if not provider_dirs:\n        return []\n\n    # Check module-level definitions\n    for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n        if isinstance(node, (ast.FunctionDef, ast.AsyncFunctionDef)):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):\n            if node.name == name:\n                return True\n        elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if isinstance(target, ast.Name) and target.id == name:\n                    return True\n\n    # Scan files for module-level dict assignments matching registry patterns\n    2. For each dict entry, verify the value references an importable callable\n    3. Unresolved references emit unwired_registry findings\n\n    Args:\n        config: Wiring analysis configuration.\n        source_dir: Root directory to scan.\n\n    Returns:\n        List of WiringFinding with finding_type=\"unwired_registry\".\n    \"\"\"\n    files, _ = _collect_python_files(source_dir, config.exclude_patterns)\n    trees: dict[Path, ast.Module] = {}\n    all_imports_by_file: dict[Path, set[str]] = {}\n\n    for f in files:\n        tree = _safe_parse(f)\n        if tree is not None:\n            trees[f] = tree\n            all_imports_by_file[f] = _extract_imports(tree)\n\n    findings: list[WiringFinding] = []\n\n    for file_path, tree in trees.items():\n        file_imports = all_imports_by_file.get(file_path, set())\n\n        for node in ast.iter_child_nodes(tree):\n            if not isinstance(node, ast.Assign):\n                continue\n\n            for target in node.targets:\n                if not isinstance(target, ast.Name):\n                    continue\n                if not _matches_registry_pattern(target.id, config.registry_patterns):\n                    continue\n\n                # \"Callable\":\n                return True\n            # Optional[Callable[...]]\n            if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Subscript):\n                if isinstance(slice_val.value, ast.Name) and annotation.value.attr == \"Optional\":\n                slice_val = annotation.slice\n                if isinstance(slice_val, ast.Name) and slice_val.id == \"Callable\":\n                    return
